   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries by infant and under-five mortality rates</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Wikipedia list article
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg/500px-Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg.png" decoding="async" width="500" height="257" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg/750px-Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e1/Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg/1000px-Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="863" data-file-height="443"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Infant_mortality_map_of_the_world.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>Infant mortality (under 1 year) rates per 1000 live births, 2013
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The under-five mortality rate is the number of deaths of infants and children under five years old per 1000 live births. The under-five mortality rate for the world is 39 deaths according to the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> and the <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a>. 5.3 million children under age five died in 2018, 14,722 every day.<sup id="cite_ref-WorldBank_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WorldBank-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The <a href="/wiki/Infant_mortality" title="Infant mortality">infant mortality</a> rate is the number of deaths of infants under one year old per 1,000 live births. This rate is often used as an indicator of the level of health in a country. The infant mortality rate of the world in 2019 was 28 according to the United Nations<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> and the projected estimate for 2020 was 30.8 according to the <i>CIA World Factbook</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-CIA-Factbook_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CIA-Factbook-5">[5]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Note that due to differences in reporting, these numbers may not be comparable across countries. The WHO recommendation is that all children who show signs of life should be recorded as live births. In many countries this standard is not followed, artificially lowering their infant mortality rates relative to countries which follow those standards. </p>
      <p><i>Note: The tables can be variously sorted using the <a href="/wiki/File:Sort_both.gif" class="image"><img alt="Sort both.gif" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/41/Sort_both.gif" decoding="async" width="21" height="9" data-file-width="21" data-file-height="9"></a> icon.</i> </p> 
      <div style="clear:both;"></div>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="OECD._Under-five_mortality_from_the_World_Bank">OECD. Under-five mortality from the World Bank</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_infant_and_under-five_mortality_rates&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: OECD. Under-five mortality from the World Bank">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The following is a list of <a href="/wiki/OECD" title="OECD">OECD</a> countries and their under-five mortality rate per 1000 live births as published by the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a>. The list has 2019 data. The OECD average was 7.0 in 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-WorldBank_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WorldBank-1">[1]</a></sup> </p>
      <p><br> </p>
